
### 3.2 Data Model

```typescript
interface Proxy {
  id: string;                    // UUID v4
  name: string;                  // User-friendly name
  host: string;                  // IP or hostname
  port: number;                  // 1-65535
  protocol: 'http' | 'https' | 'socks4' | 'socks5';
  username?: string;             // Optional auth
  password?: string;             // Encrypted
  status: 'active' | 'failed' | 'checking' | 'disabled';
  latency?: number;              // Last measured (ms)
  lastChecked?: Date;
  failureCount: number;
  totalRequests: number;
  successRate: number;
  region?: string;
  tags: string[];
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}
```

### 3.3 Key Files

| File | Purpose | Key Exports |
|------|---------|-------------|
| `electron/core/proxy-engine/manager.ts` | Main proxy orchestration | `ProxyManager` |
| `electron/core/proxy-engine/validator.ts` | Proxy health checking | `ProxyValidator` |
| `electron/core/proxy-engine/rotation.ts` | Strategy coordination | `RotationCoordinator` |
| `electron/core/proxy-engine/credential-store.ts` | Secure credential storage | `CredentialStore` |
| `electron/core/proxy-engine/strategies/*.ts` | 10+ rotation strategies | Strategy classes |

### 3.4 Integration Points

| Consumer | Integration Method | Purpose |
|----------|-------------------|---------|
| EP-003 (Tabs) | `ProxyManager.applyToSession()` | Per-tab proxy assignment |
| EP-004 (Search) | `ProxyManager.getNextProxy()` | Automatic proxy rotation |
| EP-006 (Autonomous) | `ProxyManager.recordFailure()` | Failover handling |
| EP-007 (Creator) | `ProxyManager.getNextProxy()` | Proxy for support sessions |

### 3.5 Database Tables

```sql
-- Core proxy storage
CREATE TABLE proxies (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  host TEXT NOT NULL,
  port INTEGER NOT NULL,
  protocol TEXT NOT NULL,
  username TEXT,
  password TEXT,  -- Encrypted
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'checking',
  latency INTEGER,
  last_checked DATETIME,
  failure_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  total_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  success_rate REAL DEFAULT 0,
  region TEXT,
  tags TEXT,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Rotation configuration
CREATE TABLE rotation_config (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  strategy TEXT NOT NULL,
  params TEXT,  -- JSON
  is_active INTEGER DEFAULT 1
);

-- Usage tracking for strategies
CREATE TABLE proxy_usage_stats (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  proxy_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  used_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  success INTEGER,
  latency INTEGER,
  FOREIGN KEY (proxy_id) REFERENCES proxies(id)
);
```

### 4.3 Key Files

| File | Purpose | Key Exports |
|------|---------|-------------|
| `electron/core/privacy/manager.ts` | Main privacy orchestration | `PrivacyManager` |
| `electron/core/privacy/webrtc.ts` | WebRTC leak prevention | `WebRTCShield` |
| `electron/core/privacy/tracker-blocker.ts` | Request blocking | `TrackerBlocker` |
| `electron/core/privacy/fingerprint/canvas.ts` | Canvas spoofing | `CanvasSpoofer` |
| `electron/core/privacy/fingerprint/webgl.ts` | WebGL spoofing | `WebGLSpoofer` |
| `electron/core/privacy/fingerprint/audio.ts` | Audio spoofing | `AudioSpoofer` |
| `electron/core/privacy/fingerprint/navigator.ts` | Navigator spoofing | `NavigatorSpoofer` |
| `electron/core/privacy/fingerprint/timezone.ts` | Timezone spoofing | `TimezoneSpoofer` |

### 4.4 Integration Points

| Consumer | Integration Method | Purpose |
|----------|-------------------|---------|
| EP-003 (Tabs) | `PrivacyManager.applyProtection()` | Per-tab protection |
| EP-003 (Tabs) | `PrivacyManager.generateFingerprintSeed()` | Unique identity per tab |
| EP-004 (Search) | Inherited via tabs | Anti-detection |
| EP-007 (Creator) | Inherited via tabs | Platform evasion |

---

```
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

### 5.3 Key Files

| File | Purpose | Key Exports |
|------|---------|-------------|
| `electron/core/tabs/manager.ts` | Tab lifecycle management | `TabManager` |
| `electron/core/tabs/types.ts` | Type definitions | `Tab`, `TabConfig` |

### 5.4 Integration Points

| Consumer | Integration Method | Purpose |
|----------|-------------------|---------|
| EP-001 (Proxy) | `TabManager.assignProxy()` | Per-tab proxy |
| EP-002 (Privacy) | Tab creation hooks | Apply fingerprint |
| EP-004 (Search) | `TabManager.createTab()` | Automation tabs |
| EP-007 (Creator) | `TabManager.createTab()` | Support session tabs |
| EP-010 (Session) | `TabManager.getAllTabs()` | Session persistence |

### 6.3 Key Files

| File | Purpose | Key Exports |
|------|---------|-------------|
| `electron/core/automation/manager.ts` | Main orchestration | `AutomationManager` |
| `electron/core/automation/executor.ts` | Task execution | `TaskExecutor` |
| `electron/core/automation/keyword-queue.ts` | Queue management | `KeywordQueue` |
| `electron/core/automation/search-engine.ts` | Engine abstraction | `SearchEngine` |
| `electron/core/automation/behavior-simulator.ts` | Human simulation | `BehaviorSimulator` |
| `electron/core/automation/search/result-extractor.ts` | SERP parsing | `ResultExtractor` |
| `electron/core/automation/search-rate-limiter.ts` | Rate limiting | `SearchRateLimiter` |

### 6.4 Integration Points

| Consumer | Integration Method | Purpose |
|----------|-------------------|---------|
| EP-001 (Proxy) | Uses `ProxyManager` | Proxy per search |
| EP-002 (Privacy) | Via tab creation | Anti-fingerprinting |
| EP-003 (Tabs) | Uses `TabManager` | Isolated search tabs |
| EP-005 (Domain) | Emits results | Target domain detection |
| EP-006 (Auto) | Via Scheduler | Scheduled execution |

### 6.5 Database Tables

```sql
-- Search task tracking
CREATE TABLE search_tasks (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  session_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  keyword TEXT NOT NULL,
  engine TEXT NOT NULL,
  status TEXT NOT NULL,
  proxy_id TEXT,
  tab_id TEXT,
  position INTEGER,
  results TEXT,  -- JSON
  error TEXT,
  retry_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  start_time DATETIME,
  end_time DATETIME,
  duration INTEGER,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Keyword queue persistence
CREATE TABLE keyword_queue (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  keyword TEXT NOT NULL,
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
  priority INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
```

---

### 7.3 Key Files

| File | Purpose | Key Exports |
|------|---------|-------------|
| `electron/core/automation/domain-targeting.ts` | Main domain logic | `DomainTargeting` |
| `electron/core/automation/page-interaction.ts` | Page interaction | `PageInteraction` |
| `electron/core/automation/behavior-simulator.ts` | Human behavior | `BehaviorSimulator` |
| `electron/core/automation/position-tracker.ts` | Position tracking | `PositionTracker` |

### 7.4 Database Tables

```sql
-- Target domains configuration
CREATE TABLE target_domains (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  domain TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  pattern TEXT,
  enabled INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
  priority INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  dwell_time_min INTEGER DEFAULT 30,
  dwell_time_max INTEGER DEFAULT 180,
  click_internal_links INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  last_visited DATETIME,
  visit_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  avg_position REAL,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Position history tracking
CREATE TABLE position_history (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  domain_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  keyword TEXT NOT NULL,
  engine TEXT NOT NULL,
  position INTEGER,
  found INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
  recorded_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  FOREIGN KEY (domain_id) REFERENCES target_domains(id)
);
```

---

### 8.3 Key Files

| File | Purpose | Key Exports |
|------|---------|-------------|
| `electron/core/automation/scheduler.ts` | Task scheduling | `Scheduler` |
| `electron/core/automation/self-healing-engine.ts` | Error recovery | `SelfHealingEngine` |
| `electron/core/automation/resource-monitor.ts` | System monitoring | `ResourceMonitor` |
| `electron/core/automation/cron-parser.ts` | Cron parsing | `CronParser` |
| `electron/core/automation/captcha-detector.ts` | Captcha detection | `CaptchaDetector` |
| `electron/core/resilience/circuit-breaker.ts` | Circuit breaker | `CircuitBreaker` |

### 8.4 Database Tables

```sql
-- Schedule persistence
CREATE TABLE schedules (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  name TEXT,
  type TEXT NOT NULL,  -- one-time, recurring, continuous, custom
  task_config TEXT NOT NULL,  -- JSON
  start_time DATETIME,
  end_time DATETIME,
  interval_minutes INTEGER,
  days_of_week TEXT,  -- JSON array
  cron_expression TEXT,
  enabled INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
  last_run DATETIME,
  next_run DATETIME,
  run_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Execution logs
CREATE TABLE execution_logs (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  schedule_id TEXT,
  session_id TEXT,
  status TEXT NOT NULL,
  started_at DATETIME,
  completed_at DATETIME,
  tasks_total INTEGER,
  tasks_completed INTEGER,
  tasks_failed INTEGER,
  errors TEXT,  -- JSON array
  FOREIGN KEY (schedule_id) REFERENCES schedules(id)
);
```

---


### 9.3 Key Files

| File | Purpose | Key Exports |
|------|---------|-------------|
| `electron/core/creator-support/index.ts` | Module exports | All exports |
| `electron/core/creator-support/platform-detection.ts` | Platform detection | `PlatformDetector` |
| `electron/core/creator-support/ad-viewer.ts` | Ad viewing logic | `AdViewer` |
| `electron/core/creator-support/support-tracker.ts` | Statistics tracking | `SupportTracker` |
| `electron/core/creator-support/creator-tracker.ts` | Creator management | `CreatorTracker` |
| `electron/core/creator-support/creator-scheduler.ts` | Support scheduling | `CreatorScheduler` |

### 9.4 Database Tables

```sql
-- Creator management
CREATE TABLE creators (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  url TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  platform TEXT NOT NULL,
  channel_id TEXT,
  thumbnail_url TEXT,
  subscriber_count INTEGER,
  support_methods TEXT,  -- JSON
  enabled INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
  priority INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  last_supported DATETIME,
  total_supports INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  total_ads_viewed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Support session history
CREATE TABLE support_sessions (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  creator_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  status TEXT NOT NULL,
  started_at DATETIME,
  completed_at DATETIME,
  ads_viewed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  duration_seconds INTEGER,
  proxy_id TEXT,
  FOREIGN KEY (creator_id) REFERENCES creators(id)
);

-- Individual ad impressions
CREATE TABLE ad_impressions (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  session_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  ad_type TEXT NOT NULL,
  duration_seconds INTEGER,
  completed INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
  timestamp DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  FOREIGN KEY (session_id) REFERENCES support_sessions(id)
);
```

---

### 12.2 Key Files

| File | Purpose | Key Exports |
|------|---------|-------------|
| `electron/core/session/manager.ts` | Session management | `SessionManager` |
| `src/stores/sessionStore.ts` | Frontend state | `useSessionStore` |

### 12.3 Database Tables

```sql
-- Session storage
CREATE TABLE sessions (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  tabs TEXT NOT NULL,  -- JSON array of tab configs
  window_bounds TEXT,  -- JSON {x, y, width, height}
  active_panel TEXT,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
```

### 15.2 Key Integration Interfaces

```typescript
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// SHARED INTERFACES FOR CROSS-EPIC COMMUNICATION
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

// EP-001 â†’ EP-003: Proxy Assignment
interface ProxyAssignment {
  applyToSession(session: Electron.Session, proxyId: string): Promise<void>;
  getProxyConfig(proxyId: string): ProxyConfig;
}

// EP-002 â†’ EP-003: Privacy Application
interface PrivacyApplication {
  generateFingerprintSeed(): string;
  applyProtection(webContents: WebContents, seed: string): Promise<void>;
  setWebRTCPolicy(session: Session, policy: WebRTCPolicy): void;
}

// EP-003 â†’ EP-004/005/006/007: Tab Creation for Automation
interface AutomationTabFactory {
  createAutomationTab(config: {
    url?: string;
    proxyId?: string;
    fingerprintSeed?: string;
  }): Promise<Tab>;
  closeAutomationTab(tabId: string): Promise<void>;
}

// EP-004 â†’ EP-005: Search Results Handoff
interface SearchResultsProvider {
  onResultsExtracted(callback: (results: SearchResult[]) => void): void;
  getLastResults(sessionId: string): SearchResult[];
}

// EP-006 â†’ EP-004/005/007: Scheduled Execution
interface ScheduledExecutor {
  scheduleTask(config: ScheduleConfig, task: TaskConfig): Promise<string>;
  executeNow(task: TaskConfig): Promise<void>;
}

// EP-008 â†’ EP-004: Keyword Translation
interface KeywordTranslator {
  translateKeyword(keyword: string, targetLang: string): Promise<string>;
  getLanguageForRegion(region: string): string;
}

// EP-010 â†’ EP-001/002/003: Session Persistence
interface SessionPersistence {
  captureState(): SessionState;
  restoreState(state: SessionState): Promise<void>;
}
```

### 16.2 Risk Mitigation by Epic

| Epic | Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation Strategy |
|------|------|------------|--------|---------------------|
| EP-001 | Proxy authentication failures | Medium | High | Multiple auth methods, fallback support |
| EP-002 | Fingerprint detection bypass | Medium | High | Regular updates to spoofing methods |
| EP-003 | Memory leaks with many tabs | Medium | High | Tab pool, memory monitoring, auto-cleanup |
| EP-004 | Search engine blocking | High | Medium | Human-like behavior, proxy rotation |
| EP-005 | Click detection by sites | Medium | Medium | Natural movement patterns, timing variation |
| EP-006 | Schedule reliability | Low | Medium | Persistent storage, crash recovery |
| EP-007 | Platform API changes | High | Medium | Abstracted handlers, quick update path |
| EP-008 | Translation API limits | Medium | Low | Caching, multiple providers, offline fallback |

## 17. Quick Reference

### 17.1 Epic-to-File Quick Lookup

| Epic | Main Service File | IPC Handler | UI Component | Store |
|------|-------------------|-------------|--------------|-------|
| EP-001 | `proxy-engine/manager.ts` | `handlers/tabs.ts` | `EnhancedProxyPanel.tsx` | `proxyStore.ts` |
| EP-002 | `privacy/manager.ts` | `handlers/privacy.ts` | `PrivacyPanel.tsx` | `privacyStore.ts` |
| EP-003 | `tabs/manager.ts` | `handlers/tabs.ts` | `TabBar.tsx` | (embedded) |
| EP-004 | `automation/manager.ts` | `handlers/automation.ts` | `EnhancedAutomationPanel.tsx` | `automationStore.ts` |
| EP-005 | `automation/domain-targeting.ts` | `handlers/automation.ts` | `EnhancedAutomationPanel.tsx` | `automationStore.ts` |
| EP-006 | `automation/scheduler.ts` | `handlers/automation.ts` | `EnhancedAutomationPanel.tsx` | `automationStore.ts` |
| EP-007 | `creator-support/index.ts` | `handlers/automation.ts` | `CreatorSupportPanel.tsx` | (embedded) |
| EP-008 | `translation/translator.ts` | (TBD) | (TBD) | (TBD) |
| EP-009 | (Planned) | (Planned) | (Planned) | (Planned) |
| EP-010 | `session/manager.ts` | `handlers/session.ts` | `SettingsPanel.tsx` | `sessionStore.ts` |

### 17.2 IPC Channel Reference

| Category | Channels | Handler File |
|----------|----------|--------------|
| Proxy | `proxy:add`, `proxy:remove`, `proxy:list`, `proxy:validate`, `proxy:set-rotation` | `handlers/tabs.ts` |
| Privacy | `privacy:set-webrtc`, `privacy:set-fingerprint`, `privacy:set-tracker-blocking`, `privacy:get-stats` | `handlers/privacy.ts` |
| Tabs | `tab:create`, `tab:close`, `tab:navigate`, `tab:list`, `tab:assign-proxy` | `handlers/tabs.ts` |
| Automation | `automation:start-search`, `automation:stop`, `automation:pause`, `automation:get-status` | `handlers/automation.ts` |
| Session | `session:save`, `session:load`, `session:list`, `session:delete` | `handlers/session.ts` |

### 17.3 Database Table Reference

| Epic | Tables |
|------|--------|
| EP-001 | `proxies`, `rotation_config`, `proxy_usage_stats`, `rotation_rules`, `rotation_events` |
| EP-002 | (config stored in electron-store) |
| EP-003 | (runtime only, persisted via EP-010) |
| EP-004 | `search_tasks`, `keyword_queue` |
| EP-005 | `target_domains`, `position_history` |
| EP-006 | `schedules`, `execution_logs` |
| EP-007 | `creators`, `support_sessions`, `ad_impressions` |
| EP-008 | `translation_cache` (optional) |
| EP-010 | `sessions` |

---

## 18. Avoiding Rework: Key Guidelines

### 18.1 Before Starting Any Epic

1. **Check Dependencies**: Verify all dependent epics are complete (see Section 1.1)
2. **Review Interfaces**: Understand integration interfaces (see Section 15.2)
3. **Database First**: Design and migrate database tables before coding
4. **Types First**: Define TypeScript interfaces before implementation
5. **Test Structure**: Set up test files alongside implementation

### 18.2 Common Pitfalls to Avoid

| Pitfall | Impact | Prevention |
|---------|--------|------------|
| Tight coupling between epics | Ripple changes | Use event-based communication |
| Inconsistent error handling | Unreliable recovery | Use shared circuit breaker pattern |
| Missing IPC validation | Security vulnerabilities | Always use Zod schemas |
| Direct database access | Schema changes break code | Always use repositories |
| Hardcoded values | Difficult configuration | Use constants and config files |
| Synchronous IPC | UI freezes | Always use async handlers |

### 18.3 Code Review Checklist for Epic Changes

- [ ] Does this change affect any dependent epics?
- [ ] Are all IPC channels properly rate-limited?
- [ ] Is input validation in place (Zod schemas)?
- [ ] Are database operations using repositories?
- [ ] Is error handling consistent with self-healing patterns?
- [ ] Are events properly emitted for cross-epic communication?
- [ ] Are unit tests covering the new functionality?
- [ ] Is the documentation updated?
